<th>Misc. Notes
</th>
<td>This orchestration constitutes a voiceless version of No.17 from the opera. It does not include No.8, the "Dance of the Polovetsian Maidens" (F major, 6/8). This score was also issued by <a href="/wiki/M.P._Belaieff" title="M.P. Belaieff">M.P. Belaieff</a>, <a href="/wiki/Universal_Edition" title="Universal Edition">Universal Edition</a> (Philharmonia), and <a href="/wiki/Boosey_%26_Hawkes" title="Boosey &amp; Hawkes">Boosey &amp; Hawkes</a>. Kalmus' 1933 copyright claim is bogus.

<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>The opera was incomplete at Borodin's death. It was completed and mostly orchestrated by <a href="/wiki/Category:Rimsky-Korsakov,_Nikolay" title="Category:Rimsky-Korsakov, Nikolay">Nikolay Rimsky-Korsakov</a> and <a href="/wiki/Category:Glazunov,_Aleksandr" title="Category:Glazunov, Aleksandr">Aleksandr Glazunov</a>.
